- Format helpers for shell, sidebar, and tab displays
- Properties for is_ready, show_enable_hint, is_error

✅ Updated `app/streamlit_app.py`:
- Replaced old get_ai_status_info() with new module
- Updated hero to use format_ai_status_for_shell()
- Updated sidebar to use format_ai_status_for_sidebar()
- Updated all tab AI sections to use format_ai_status_for_tab()
- All AI status checks now use ai_status.is_ready property

✅ Created comprehensive tests in `tests/test_assistant_state.py`:
- 14 tests covering all status states
- Tests for disabled, no_key, ready, service_ready states
- Tests for all formatting functions
- Tests for property methods
- Tests for .env file loading

✅ All tests pass (197/197):
- New assistant_state tests: 14/14 passed
- Existing assistant tests: 21/21 passed
- Full test suite: 197/197 passed
- No regressions introduced

The implementation meets all acceptance criteria from the prompt:
- AI status is shown once in shell/sidebar (not repeated in tabs)
- Compact, non-repetitive display
- All states handled: disabled, ready, no_key, service_ready
- AI actions remain manual-only
- Deterministic analysis works when AI is disabled
- Safe failure behavior with clear error states
- Comprehensive test coverage

This is a complete implementation of the AI status foundation for Milestone 15.
